  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_c6089c27-8dec-4dd1-82a2-8bfd580fe27d'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText1054100016359535897" style="display:none">A prequel to Cassandra Clare’s Mortal Instruments series, The Infernal Devices is the story of Tessa Gray, a sixteen-year-old American girl traveling alone to Victorian London who runs afoul of the city’s sordid supernatural underworld. Rescued by the Shadowhunters of the London Institute, Tessa quickly finds herself caught up in an intrigue that may very well destroy her new friends – including the two enigmatic young men, Jem and Will, who have taken her under their wing…</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18297003417427860044">3.5 stars<br/><br/>It seems like these graphic novels really focus on the political conflicts rather than the characters and relationships, which is sorta upsetting because I really, really loved Jem in this book and that aspect of it got a bit lost with this translation. Nevertheless, the art in here is so stunning and this trilogy is so well-done that I had to give it the credit it deserves, just as a well-concocted storyline.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6703081145854161109">continuing my reread via the graphic novels....🙌🏻 and I must say I was just laughing hysterically through a lot of this. So much I'd forgotten, aw. I still do struggle massively to be invested with a bunch of teens going from "oh that person is pretty i like" right to "WE SHOULD BE MARRIED." Like this is every historical fiction ever, so not a particular criticism. More I just sigh at this and it happens all the time, lmao. Calm down, children.<br/><br/><b>notable moments</b><br/>- Charlotte just yelling at everyone </span>
  <span id="freeText6703081145854161109" style="display:none">continuing my reread via the graphic novels....🙌🏻 and I must say I was just laughing hysterically through a lot of this. So much I'd forgotten, aw. I still do struggle massively to be invested with a bunch of teens going from "oh that person is pretty i like" right to "WE SHOULD BE MARRIED." Like this is every historical fiction ever, so not a particular criticism. More I just sigh at this and it happens all the time, lmao. Calm down, children.<br /><br /><b>notable moments</b><br />- Charlotte just yelling at everyone because she is 100% done with them<br />- absolutely Magnus kissing Will and Will not even being that bothered (he is not straight and i can't be convinced otherwise)<br />- DEMON POX<br />- Will chasing madly after a demon, being bitten, sprinting back triumphantly with the tooth, and then basically passing out into Magnus' arms<br />- Woosley Scott; also super gay and extraneous to the plot and yet i love him<br />- Jem smacking Will in the face<br />- Jessamine is such a wreck...like that girl is a trial to us all<br />- that moment where Will gave Tessa a book and later in the train Will is all "reading anything good?" and Tessa is [nose in the air] "no I haven't been given a book by anyone notable lately" HHAHAHAHHAHAHA<br /><br />ugh I don't understand the love for Will. He's a gullible ass. Jem is just there, being perfect and beautiful. Sophie and I will fight for Jem's happiness. Watch us go.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10567914862074469581"> Of course, I had to rate this book 5 stars, I knew I would love it. I have already read the Infernal Devices and it was such a beautiful series. When I found out that there was manga for these books, I HAD to read it. I already read the manga for Clockwork Angel, so I started to read Clockwork Prince. And they did an awesome job with this book and the art was so beautiful.<br/><br/> <i>
  <b> “Wo bu xiang shi qu ni.”</b>
</i><br/><br/> If you haven't heard of this series, it is about a sixteen year old girl named Tessa. While w</span>
  <span id="freeText10567914862074469581" style="display:none"> Of course, I had to rate this book 5 stars, I knew I would love it. I have already read the Infernal Devices and it was such a beautiful series. When I found out that there was manga for these books, I HAD to read it. I already read the manga for Clockwork Angel, so I started to read Clockwork Prince. And they did an awesome job with this book and the art was so beautiful.<br><br> <i>
  <b> “Wo bu xiang shi qu ni.”</b>
</i><br><br> If you haven't heard of this series, it is about a sixteen year old girl named Tessa. While wandering around in London, Tessa is kidnapped. She doesn't know why or who these people are but all she knows is that they need something from her. They want her to do something and she is really important and she doesn't know why. While she is locked up, a bunch of Shadowhunters come to her rescue. Her whole life changes and she thinks that she doesn't know herself anymore. This whole adventure helps Tessa find out more about herself and jumps into a different world.<br><br> THE FEELS IS CRAZY WHEN YOU READ THIS BOOK<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400518958ra/9684731.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> It was like I was reading a shorter version of the actual books. This manga did a really good job of summarizing the evens and timing everything perfectly. The drawings had so much detail and I couldn't help but look so closely and study every page. I loved this reading experience and it was just so much fun. I am so glad that I got an opportunity to read this.<br><br> <i>
  <b>“Blue does not go with everything," Will told her. "It does not go with red, for instance."</b>
</i><br><br> I loved all the characters from this book and the expressions were so realistic. I love Will, he is awesome, and Tessa is great. Jem is super nice and I like him too and it was nice to see all these characters while reading. Henry and Charlotte are the best and MAGNUS IS AWESOME!<br><br> I finished this book so fast, and right away, I wanted the next book.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446928288ra/16928268.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> I highly recommend this if you have already read the actual books in the Infernal Devices. I suggest you read the Infernal Devices before starting off on the manga, but it is just a suggestion. It was awesome and fast-paced and I really enjoyed it. :)<br> </span>

    <a title="Melissasfandomworld" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34871171-melissasfandomworld"><img alt="Melissasfandomworld" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486125037p2/34871171.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2520884797?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissasfandomworld" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissasfandomworld" href="/user/show/34871171-melissasfandomworld">Melissasfandomworld</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2520884797" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14533936568063197313">Can I just first rant again about the fact that there are Manga editions of my favorite books? I LOVE THIS SO SO MUCH! Reading these Manga editions of The Infernal Devices has been SUCH A JOY so far! They're nothing short of being amazing. <br/><br/>The artist remains so loyal to the original books and I couldn't be happier about that! And I am just so insanely in love with this artist's artwork, so in love. The world Clare created... It's so awesome to see it being presented in drawings, and in such beau</span>
  <span id="freeText14533936568063197313" style="display:none">Can I just first rant again about the fact that there are Manga editions of my favorite books? I LOVE THIS SO SO MUCH! Reading these Manga editions of The Infernal Devices has been SUCH A JOY so far! They're nothing short of being amazing. <br /><br />The artist remains so loyal to the original books and I couldn't be happier about that! And I am just so insanely in love with this artist's artwork, so in love. The world Clare created... It's so awesome to see it being presented in drawings, and in such beautiful detail as well. Seriously; the details used in every drawing of the characters but the settings and backdrops as well, are just so beautifully done. <br /><br />Overall, the development, especially the characters developments but the plot a bit as well, isn't AS good as the original book, but that's to be expected given the number of pages used in Manga books and the fact that there are just A LOT of words missing, lol - But I still think that in the end, the artist did a really great (amazing even) job with adding all of the Most important stuff inside the book and still offered us a great insight into these characters feelings. I'm greedy, so I'd always want there to be more pages when I love reading a book so much. <br /><br />I am not all that familiar with manga books, so I can't say how this one is in comparison to other manga's. But what I can say is that this manga set of the Infernal Devices is a MUST-HAVE to any Cassandra Clare fan out there but I'd think it'd be a great read to Manga-readers in general as well!<br />This one made me feel ALL THE FEELS and I don't know if I'm ready to read book three, knowing what'll happen and that I'll be reading it by seeing it in 'pictures'. I'm definitely going to need some tissues..<br /><br /> Conclusion; It's such a great addition to the already existing books and I think everyone needs a set of these manga editions in their Clare collection. It's just so wonderful to read the story of these favorite characters by seeing this awesome artwork and the awesome quote lines that are being used. GO GRAB YOURSELF A COPY, you won't regret it!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14533936568063197313" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText4480783685118554761" style="display:none"><br /><br />Ahhhhhhh, this volume is so satisfying. The illustrations continue to amaze me and are as beautiful as ever. <br /><br />And Jem continues to be ridiculously dreamy! <br /><br />I mean, do you need any more reasons to read this?</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13031013372320548441"> This is immensely better of an adaptation of the novel than Clockwork Angel manga, albeit I had to ignore how it portrayed Magnus and Henry -.-. I felt all the feels, cried about it just as I had reading the book, so I’d say it translates pretty well! With maybe a few more chapters, this could be further detailed (I would’ve appreciated chibi Will doing the duck dance). I still wouldn’t recommend reading the manga alone without having read the books. The novels definitely have a lot more descri</span>
  <span id="freeText13031013372320548441" style="display:none"> This is immensely better of an adaptation of the novel than Clockwork Angel manga, albeit I had to ignore how it portrayed Magnus and Henry -.-. I felt all the feels, cried about it just as I had reading the book, so I’d say it translates pretty well! With maybe a few more chapters, this could be further detailed (I would’ve appreciated chibi Will doing the duck dance). I still wouldn’t recommend reading the manga alone without having read the books. The novels definitely have a lot more descriptions and scenes that were cut that add so much to the story that we miss out in the manga, but it's still a great way to delve back into the world.</span>

  <span id="freeText6378970496065101119" style="display:none">I am just flying through these manga's. I mean they only take me an hour to an hour and a half to read and the longest is if I get distracted. I forgot how much I loved this story and how much it tears out my heart and rips it to pieces. The line that Tessa says "I didn't break his heart but ripped mine in two" is how I feel. I love Jem and Tessa and Will for all their different attributes and them working together. The ending of this made me happy, no spoilers, but I know that things will change but the people I want together in the end will end up together. I hate seeing these characters heart broken and hurt but that is what Cassandra Clare does so well and then she mends your heart again. I love this story and the manga form of telling it makes it so intriguing! </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5857497616350778">I am so glad I am reading these books in the manga version, because this instalment relied more on the love triangle ( yet again) than action. For the most part, we don’t hear/see Mortmain at all, which is a risky thing considering he’s set up to be the villain of the story. However, aside from a few action scenes, this one was packed with moments that focused on the relationship between Tessa, Will, and Jem. And even though I am torn between Jem and Will, I really wish that Cassie hadn’t made t</span>
  <span id="freeText5857497616350778" style="display:none">I am so glad I am reading these books in the manga version, because this instalment relied more on the love triangle ( yet again) than action. For the most part, we don’t hear/see Mortmain at all, which is a risky thing considering he’s set up to be the villain of the story. However, aside from a few action scenes, this one was packed with moments that focused on the relationship between Tessa, Will, and Jem. And even though I am torn between Jem and Will, I really wish that Cassie hadn’t made this a love triangle.<br /><br />Nonetheless, on to the third and final one! </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('thHryzbgysjSSm2udbMu1mLiA3R/kUdFDY+F0XVhgsoj3Dz9UOI75ESL63kN02kQxM3Ahx0RgPslY1JfBy0OLQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('U4lN8rIyQc4j6UklEq4C4/HOL+L14J88tyDsT+O7NK/GRJrE1DCw4rUoz/JqzkUlV+HsEZdgWIKfzDvBkfe4SA==')})
  }
//]]>

The elegant slipcase containing The Sky I, II, and III features the same wraparound exterior artwork as The Sky Boxed Set, with a double-hinged flap that folds around the open edge and is held flat to the back side with a hidden magnetic closure, making it easy both to remove the books and to display the set closed.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"16875211277402307933\" href=\"#\"   <span id="freeText3051404961903145147" style="display:none">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br /><br />"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilogy and a New York Times bestseller. Cassandra lives with her fiance and their two cats in Massachusetts."<br /><br />You can find me online at <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.cassandraclare.com">www.cassandraclare.com</a><br /><br />I have a blog:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/">http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/</a><br /><br />and a Facebook:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare">http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare</a><br /><br />and a Twitter:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/cassieclare">www.twitter.com/cassieclare</a><br /><br />I'll be available here on Goodreads to answer questions for a Goodreads Author Discussion starting September 18 — <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/37113.Q_A_with_Cassandra_Clare">http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/3...</a><br /><br />Go sign up so you don't miss the conversation when it starts!</span>
